The chickens decide to attempt an escape so they don't get turned into chicken pot pies.">

        var mps = mps||{}; mps._queue = mps._queue||{}; mps._queue.gptloaded = mps._queue.gptloaded||[];
        mps._queue.gptloaded.push(function () {
            mps.insertAd('#super_movie_tv_ad','superdetail');
        });
    </script>

        <h2 class=" panel-heading what-to-know__header">What to know</h2>
        <div class="what-to-know__body">
            <section>
                <h3 class="what-to-know__section-title">
                    <score-icon-critic
                        size="tiny"
                        percentage="hide"
                        state="certified-fresh"

                </h3>
                <p class="what-to-know__section-body">
                    <span data-qa="critics-consensus"><em>Chicken Run</em> has all the charm of Nick Park's <em>Wallace & Gromit</em>, and something for everybody. The voice acting is fabulous, the slapstick is brilliant, and the action sequences are spectacular.</span>
                    <a href="/m/chicken_run/reviews?intcmp=rt-what-to-know_read-critics-reviews">Read critic reviews</a>
                </p>
            </section>
            
        </div>
    </section>

    <script>
        var mps = mps || {};
        mps._queue = mps._queue || {};
        mps._queue.gptloaded = mps._queue.gptloaded || [];
        mps._queue.adload = mps._queue.adload || [];

        mps._queue.gptloaded.push(function() {
            if (mps.getResponsiveSet() =='0') { //MOBILE
                mps.insertAd('#interscroller_ad','interscroller');
            }
        });
        mps._queue.adload.push(function(eo) {
            if (eo._mps._slot === 'interscroller' && eo.isEmpty) {
                document.querySelector('.mobile-interscroller').classList.add('isEmpty');
            }
        });
    </script>

    <h2 class="panel-heading">Audience Reviews for <em>Chicken Run</em></h2>
    
        
        <div class="sr-only js-clamp-live-region" aria-live="polite"></div>
        <ul class="mop-audience-reviews__reviews-wrap clearfix">
            
            
            
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">

                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__half "></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Nov 23, 2014</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">A great escape movie that&#39;s basically a showcase for Nick Park&#39;s love of highly elaborate contraptions and genre mash-ups/references. Also, it&#39;s nice to see a children&#39;s movie where the main hero is a woman (granted she&#39;s a chicken, but let&#39;s not split hairs on this).</div>

                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">The stop-motion animation is impressive with well-executed action sequences to boost. Unfortunately, the story treads on too much familiar ground and tends to feel too mellow at times.  The characters do a good job for the purposes they serve even though not one is particularly memorable.  Despite some really good moments of humor, this film fails to be as endearing as Wallace and Gromit, another Aardman Animation effort.</div>
